# Forgotten Ones | Bluebook Wes 1

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (01/27/2024 03:15:15) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1200640136698937364"></a>*1200640136698937364*

Wes has made his way to Fakir via a cargo hauler acting as a member of the crew where he has been tasked to collect intelligence pertaining to rumors of Seperatist activity on the planet from an agent at an arranged meeting place - a hired room in the back of a seedy cantina known as the Legs Akimbo, famous mainly for its dancing girls and rough clientele... but also known in underground circles for privacy and discretion.  
In addition to collecting the information,  he was provided with an encrypted data card to hand over to his contact.
No details regarding the contact were provided other than they would be wearing a green jacket with a black armband.

---

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (01/27/2024 03:27:52) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1200643310121930822"></a>*1200643310121930822*

((OK.  I'm going to leave it open to set yourself up. This is going to be fairly open ended though I do have a goal in mind. Time period is going to be about 3 months before the end of the war.))

---

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (01/30/2024 17:19:54) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1201939863449124964"></a>*1201939863449124964*

Wes entered theough the threshold and took in the atmosphere of the cantina.   *Legs Akimbo* wasn’t much different than most other establishments that ran along the same lines.  Just change the planet and the name and there you were.  


What struck him first was the noise and the band and the dancing girls that were on the stage.   No doubt causing patrons who were already inebriated to soon part with their credits even faster.   


Turning his armored head to the right he stepped off the somewhat lit entrance into the dim, smoky interior of the cantina.   The loud music and background noise of patrons from across the galaxy grounded out the armored footfalls he made.    


This was one time he was glad people saw the armor and not the sixteen year old teen underneath.  While wasn’t his first time alone on a mission this was his first time alone with no backup clan mates on the planet.   


It was time to grow up.  So to speak.  


Making his way to the bar he flagged the bartender and ordered whatever passed for a local brew and then turned around to take in the scene before him.   


He did not know who or what the contact was.  Only that they would be wearing a green jacket with a black armband.

---

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (01/30/2024 18:05:43) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1201951394949767199"></a>*1201951394949767199*

The patrons of the *Legs Akimbo* consist of a variety of aliens, though are predominantly the local species the Fakiri, a Human offshoot who are at least a half a meter shorter on average. Looking closer Wes discovers number of the non natives wear a black armband, however none of them sport a green jacket. 
In addition to the entertainment, a few tables of Sabaac and other gambling ventures can be spotted towards one corner of the room. The noise from these tables competes with the 'music' from the band. 
During one particularly loud celebration from one of the games a slight figure slips in towards the bar, leaning against it as the young Human woman catches the bartender's attention.
The Fakiri nods to her in recognition and greeting, "**Usual, Rin?**"
"**Ya, thanks,**" she turns to assess the happenings around her, her gaze lingering on Wes for slightly longer than the others. From his vantage as she turns, he can see the black armband over her dark green jacket. 
Behind her the bartender sets her usual order down on the counter. "**Drisk was looking for you earlier.**"
Turning her attention away from the patrons she picks up her drink and eyes the bartender. "**Was he now,**" her tone is matter of fact as if she anticipated the development. 
The bartender's eyes narrow at the young woman and he looks as if he's going to start a lecture, but instead takes the credits she tosses on the counter before walking away.
The woman goes back to her survey of the cantina, her dark blue gaze coming back to rest on Wes before giving him a small incline of her head in acknowledgment. Waylaying any interaction with Wes in the main room, she takes her drink and heads towards the back.

---

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (01/30/2024 23:59:00) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1202040301913645056"></a>*1202040301913645056*

Wes looked about the cantina.   There was a lot going on and it would be easy to miss something if one wasn’t watching for it.  Wes was beginning to understand why this place was favored for meets like this.   


According to the chrono in his helmet five minutes had passed and he was beginning to wonder when the contact would arrive.   


He started to turn towards the bar and the drink that had been set there for him.  When he spotted a woman in a dark green jacket.   He did his best to listen despite the competing background noise.  She had a quick exchange of words with the bartender.  Wes believed he caught her name.   


The rest happened quickly.  The lingering glance and slight nod in his direction.   The black armband stood out in contrast to the dark green jacket she wore.  


Another name was mentioned between the two as Wes appeared to be looking out over the crowd.  Turning his gaze back her way he sees her dark blue eyes upon him.  Seeing the incline of her head Wes knew he had met the contact he was supposed to.    He watched the woman walk off towards the back preventing any communication out in the open.  


The Mandalorian tagged her in his HUD as he grabbed his drink and waited.  After a short moment he pushed away from the bar and made his way slowly towards the woman named Rin.  


The farther back he went the loud ruckus of the cantina dropped slightly.  Seeing where Rin was seated he made his way over to her giving her a slight nod as he sat down across from her.

---

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (01/31/2024 00:30:15) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1202048163813543956"></a>*1202048163813543956*

Wes finds the woman, Rin, is not much older than he as he sits across from her at the table.  Her gaze is piercing in its intensity as she watches him approach and join her. With the back of her hand, she sweeps a lock of her dark brown hair futily behind her ear only for it to escape once more as she sips from her glass.
After a long moment, she pulls out a small device and places it between them on the table before activating it.  Around the pair, all outside noise stops and Wes can assume anyone wanting to listen in now can't thanks to the sound sponge. She draws it under the table again and out of sight.  "**I wasn't expecting for them to send a Mandalorian,**" she says evenly, taking a sip of her drink. "**Have to say that's  a first.**"

---

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (01/31/2024 17:30:29) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1202304916979191828"></a>*1202304916979191828*

Sitting across from the woman Wes took note of her eyes.  They were dangerous in more ways than one.  He also realized that she wasn’t much older than he was.    This war had caused what should have been kids enjoying their youth into combatants.  


He watched her fight with a lock of dark hair in a futile attempt to keep it behind her ear.   It was as if it had a mind of its own and wanted to be free.  


With her quick use of a sound sponge their space became as quiet as can be.   Since his helmet knocked the decibels down some it was even more quiet.  He could hear himself breathing as she spoke.   


He nodded as he reached up and removed his helmet, setting it aside on the table.   His short brownish hair along with brown eyes were now visible to the young woman.    Wes may have looked sixteen but his eyes spoke a different story.   


**”I wasn’t sure what to expect either.  I wasn’t told who or what my contact would be.  Seems that today is a day of firsts for both of us.”**


He reached for his drink and took his first taste of it.  **”I will say this, this is one of the better places I’ve had to meet a contact.”**

---

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (01/31/2024 17:48:30) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1202309450854043708"></a>*1202309450854043708*

Rin watches as he removes his helmet, surprise showing in her expression before she schools it. "**This place has it's uses. It's one of a few places that allows off-worlders.**" She adds with a shrug, "**The Fakiri can be a bit xenophobic and like to keep tabs on who comes and goes.**" She glances for a moment in the direction of the main room before turning her attention back to Wes.
 "**Where you given my orders?**" she asks getting down to the business at hand.

---

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (01/31/2024 19:06:32) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1202329086563987476"></a>*1202329086563987476*

Wes gave her a half smile when he saw her reaction of seeing him without his helmet.  He listens to her explain the Fakiri and their xenophobic tendencies.   


When she glanced out to the main room Wes followed with his own gaze and took a look at what she may be booking at or for.  Weather anything was there or not she quickly looked back.   The movement caused that same lock of hair to come loose again from her ear.  Causing him to give her a slight smile.  


She quickly got to the business at hand.  


**”Yes I was.”**  He answered matter of factly as he reached to his utility belt and removed the data card from one of its compartments.  


He placed it in the middle of the table between them.  **”How active has the war been here?”**

---

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (01/31/2024 19:28:18) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1202334565369122857"></a>*1202334565369122857*

Picking up the card, Rin eyes it thoughtfully before apparently being satisfied with it's validity. Pulling up the cuff of one sleeve she reveals a miniaturized bracer computer and inserts the card. With a tap of a finger she begins the decryption. **"Not very. The Fakiri maintain their neutrality in the conflict.**" 
Resting her elbows on the table she steeples her fingers in front of her.
"**At least on the surface. Behind closed doors they've been meeting with Seperatist representatives and have allowed them to occupy a stronghold outside of town.**"
Checking the bracer when it beeps, her thoughts turn to the contents her eyes moving as she reads the display. "**Oh... the kriffing bastard,**" she says under her breath, apparently not please at all by the contents.

---

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (01/31/2024 21:35:48) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1202366651769557013"></a>*1202366651769557013*

She confirmed what had long been thought. That the Fakiri had been secretly working with the separatists.  Wes had heard the rumors.   Apparently they weren’t caring about keeping it quiet anymore.  Xenophobic or not that was going to get out.   


He watched her read the file.   Her eyes darted back and forth quickly.   Her exclamation confirmed what her face had been telling him as she read.   She wasn’t happy.  


**”Let me guess.   Not what you wanted to read?    How bad?”**  He wasn’t sure if she would answer but he figured it was worth a shot.

---

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (01/31/2024 22:59:36) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1202387740944109589"></a>*1202387740944109589*

A part of Rin hears the question directed at her but she doesn't acknowledge it as her own thoughts seem to be taking in the latest piece of news. As she's about to respond to him her attention instead snaps to the main room.
“**Put your helmet on,**” she says shortly. “**Don't get involved… if you can help it.**” The last is said with a bit of a smirk as she turns off the sound sponge and calmly picks up her juma juice.
Wes has little time to respond before a dark shadow looms over their booth. Standing over them is a dark furred Togorian, his fists clenching and unclenching in bridled fury as he looks down at his prey.
“**I’ve found you, little girl,**” the voice belonging to the menacing Togorian booms, his fists clenching.

---

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (02/01/2024 00:32:14) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1202411050625138780"></a>*1202411050625138780*

He watched her reread the news on the data chip.  He was beginning to wonder just what was on it but he never got the chance to ask again.  She looked quickly back to the main floor and was quick to hurry him to put his helmet back on.   


Hearing the tone in her voice he didn’t hesitate to do as told.  Her second quip was said with a slight smirk.  *Does she know me?*  The young Mandalorian thought to himself, deciding that he rather enjoyed the smirk she gave him.    


He was about to respond when she turned off the sound sponge.  The loud drumming noise of the cantina came back to the both of them and that wasn't the only thing.   A large dark shadow suddenly loomed over both of them.  Wes glanced up at the large alien and then back to Rin.   His expressionless helmet looked at the young woman as the deep bass voice of the Togorian booms out.  *‘I’ve found you little girl.’*


Wes reached for his drink and moved it to the side with his left hand.    His head turned slightly towards the Togorian as his right hand left the table.    He waited to see where this was going.  He took in their immediate surroundings.

---

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (02/01/2024 01:50:33) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1202430761484034058"></a>*1202430761484034058*

“**And a remarkable job at that…**” Rin quips, if the Togorian’s imposing figure is affecting her she gives no sign. “**Now why don’t you go away and come looking for me another time.**”
With a growl, the Togorian grabs Rin by the front of her jacket and yanks her from the booth. She gives a small yelp of surprise, apparently having not expected the development.  “**You have something of mine.**”
“**I can understand your confusion… you really should watch what you bet.**“ Her words only reward her with the Togorian lifting her further off the ground. From his vantage Wes can see her reaching into her jacket. “**Now if you're done, I think we can make a deal.**”
“**Deal?**,” he snarls, not moving to lower Rin.
“**Yes, your sc'rath in exchange for a meeting with your employer at the Annex.**”
He blinks at her for a moment, his mouth turning up with a snarl. Suddenly the Togorian drops Rin to her feet, which she surprisingly lands before taking a cautious step back. “**Fine,**” he growls, showing Rin his sharp teeth. “**I'll find you when it's done.**”
Wisely Rin just gives the Togorian a nod in response and watches as the large alien turns and departs before returning to the booth. She picks up her cup and drains it.
“**That went well.**”

---

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (02/01/2024 19:50:11) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1202702459865399346"></a>*1202702459865399346*

Wes watched the exchange between Rin and the Togorian.  He wasn’t surprised when she was picked up by the large alien.    Despite being held in the air she still seemed to somewhat be in control.   


He wasn’t sure if her talk of a deal tripped up the alien or if it was actually something that would work out for him.   Either way it had the desired effect as lands taking a step back.    


He shifted, relaxing slightly.   His hand, still resting on his holstered blaster, was under the table.   


With the impromptu meeting between the diminutive Rin and the hulking Togorian now over, Wes nodded at the woman.   Unknown to Rin he was smiling beneath his helmet when she said that it had gone well.  


**”Did it now?  There seemed to be some quick bargaining going on.  Did it buy you the time you…”**  He pauses for a quick second.  **”…Or we need?”**

---

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (02/01/2024 20:01:59) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1202705428866277418"></a>*1202705428866277418*

Rin hmms as she glances back toward the main room to make sure the Togorian was out of ear shot. “**I’ve been setting this up for a couple weeks now. He’s honor bound to get his sc’rath back so he’ll do what I want,**” she gives a small smile that doesn’t match the sudden glint in her eyes. “**And then I’ll be able to get into the Separatist base.**”
Growing somber she then adds, “**I had expected to be sent backup for this next stage, but apparently my er... partner was sent on another mission.**”

---

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (02/01/2024 21:08:50) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1202722253046030487"></a>*1202722253046030487*

Wes saw the somber look on her face as she mentioned a partner being sent somewhere else.   Going into a separatist installation alone wasn’t a good way to prolong one’s future.   


He leaned forward since they didn’t have the sound dampening field up and running.  **”Look, I don't have to return right away.  If you need help, I’ll do what I can.  We’re fighting the same fight.”** 


He leaned back slightly.   **”I’m Wes Del’Fin.”**  He introduced himself.

---

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (02/01/2024 22:43:25) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1202746054882099240"></a>*1202746054882099240*

Rin's head inclines to the side in acknowledgment. "**Everyone here knows me as Rin Draay,**" she says, obviously providing only her cover name. She seems to take a moment to consider his offer as she slides her now empty cup from one hand to another in front of her.
“**I don't know. I work a particular way and I need someone who can keep up to watch my back.**” Rin stops shifting the cup as she looks over Wes, assessing him. “**If what I’ve heard about a Mandalorian's training is true, then you may do.**” There seems to be a part of Rin that finds the idea of the two of them working together amusing. 
Searching through one of her pouches she locates a scrap piece of flimsiplast and stylus. Her focus turns to writing on it in a neat script.
“**This is where you can find me once you get your affairs in order,**” she says, sliding the flimsi towards him. “**Don't worry about finding lodgings, there's an extra room,**" she indicates the flimsiplast before moving to leave. "**I have some work to take care of and I'll be there later.**”
On the flimsiplast is an address and what looks like an access code.

---

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (02/02/2024 15:52:53) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1203005127011864676"></a>*1203005127011864676*

Wes smiled beneath his helmet as she commented about Mandalorian training and that he may be able to keep up.  **”What you’ve heard is probably only half of it.   Rest assured I’ll keep up just fine.”**  A bit of youthful cockyness entered his voice.  It wasn’t often that his ability was questioned.  He rather enjoyed it from Rin.   


Taking the offered flimsiplast from her he listened as she laid out the quick plan for meeting there soon.   He nodded and stood up from the table watching her walk away quickly.   ***This is going to be interesting.***  He thought and he started to casually make his way out of the cantina and to the meeting place.

---

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (02/02/2024 16:24:20) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1203013043827777566"></a>*1203013043827777566*

The address Rin provided takes Wes into what is apparently a residential district with an assortment of multi-family dwellings. The particular dwelling is set off via an alley from the main street and while well maintained has the look of being set up as affordable housing. Finding the particular unit, one of eight in this building, Wes is able to punch in the access code Rin provides for him before entering.
The apartment itself has been sparsely furnished and there’s very little decoration. By all appearances, the apartment came furnished and the occupants felt it was suitable enough without adding to it. The only sign of mess is off to one side on a table that’s been set up holding a variety of parts. None of which seem to go together to resemble anything Wes would be familiar with.

The first room consists of the living area, a dining nook and the kitchen. From there Wes finds doors that lead into a pair of bedrooms and a refresher between them. One room has obviously been claimed by Rin by the size and style of the extra clothing he finds. The other has been untouched for a while, but has been left neat. Spare clothing for a man hang in the wardrobe.

It’s a few hours before Rin returns, the sun starting to set.

---

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (02/02/2024 17:17:18) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1203026371807416340"></a>*1203026371807416340*

Wes found his way to the dwelling with little problem.  It was fairly nondescript as places come.  Which was a good thing.  Too flashy brought attention.   Not that a Mandalorian walking anywhere didn’t bring attention.    Either way he quickly made his way into the building.   


Inside was pretty much what he expected.   Cleaned and organized.  He saw the one room that he figured was Rin’s.   Respecting her privacy he left the room and claimed the one that looked unoccupied.  Looking around at the rest of the rooms he concluded that he was safe here for the time being.   He relaxed his awareness some as he removed his helmet and looked around the kitchen.   He helped himself to some quick snacks.   


It had been a bit and since he had the time he set about cleaning himself up as best he could.  By the time Rin had arrived the sun had started to set.   Upon entering she saw Wes at the table, blaster in hand.    He set it down seeing that it was her coming through the entryway.  The upper half of his armor was off as he set back to finishing the maintenance on the chest and back coverings.  


Holding it up he nodded and looked at Rin.  **”Welcome back.   Everything coming together?”**

---

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (02/02/2024 19:00:05) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1203052240265289799"></a>*1203052240265289799*

Rin is deep in thought as she enters the apartment, carrying a bag of something quite fragrant. She hmms in response, still apparently trying to reconcile something as she takes the bag and sets it on the table. “**It’s a long game. Things have a way of working themselves out,**” she says at last. 
Finally taking in the scene in front of her she glances at the armor plates he had removed to maintain and then him, her expression unreadable for a moment. 
“**I brought some dinner. Help yourself,**” she gestures to the bag. “**I’m going to get cleaned up.**”

---

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (02/02/2024 19:29:10) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1203059556633022514"></a>*1203059556633022514*

He nodded at her response.  Can’t rush a plan.  He knew that better than most.    When she stopped talking he looked at her.  He saw her looking at the armor he had removed and laid out on the table.   He saw her gaze shift from the table to him.   He gave her a smile as she talked about dinner and cleaning up.   


It was then that the smell of the food had arrived at his nose and he realized just how hungry he was.    **”Yeah go ahead Rin.  I already did that myself.”** He said quickly as he took off the remaining armor covering his thighs and shins.  This left him in the dark gray spandex bodysuit he wore under his armor.  Despite covering him from ankles to wrists it was form fitting.    There wasn’t much modesty growing up Mandalorian.  He sometimes forgot that.   **”I hope you don’t mind?**”  He added as he moved to the food.  


**”This smells good.  I’m not sure I could tell you when I last had a hot meal.”** He called out as he helped himself to a modest helping of the good smelling food. 


Sitting back down he went back to work on his armor as he ate.   By the time Rin returned his plate was half consumed and he was now going over his blaster.   He gave her a smile.

The act of taking her hand caused them to both turn and face each other.   Closer now, if it was possible, then when she had just walked past.  Her hair was still slightly damp and that rogue strand of hair had broken loose of its hold.  He now realized how much taller he was.  


He looked from her hand that he held into her deep blue eyes.  His own dark eyes searched hers.   She felt the fingers of his other hand gently touch the scars on her tone arm.  He slowly traced fingers from one scar to another.  The feeling of electricity only intensified for him.    


Words escaped him as he let out a deep breath he didn’t realize he was holding.  Fingers left her arm and traveled up finally tucking the rogue hair behind her ear.   Wes looked into her blue eyes again and a small smile crossed his face.

Rin's posture tenses as he grabs her hand and an unreadable expression crosses her features as his grasp turns them to face each other. His touch sends their own wave of electricity through her causing her to shudder releasing the tension. As their eyes meet, he can see the internal conflict reflect back at him.

Suddenly tensing once more she pushes back on his chest and tries to remove her hand from his grasp. “**No… We… I can't,**” she corrects knowing it wasn't his fault they weren't about to act on what was apparently a mutual attraction. “**I'm sorry,**” she adds with sincere regret, moving to take a step backward towards her room.

## **yogi_001** (02/04/2024 21:02:40) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1203807865777688616"></a>*1203807865777688616*

Wes could see the emotions running a course as he looked into her ever so blue eyes.    There was an attraction that not only he felt.  When he fell her hand on his chest his own breath sharpened as the sensation of electricity intensified between them.  


It seemed that she felt it too.   Feeling her tensing as he tucked her hair he felt the slight push on his chest.   He not only saw the conflict in her eyes he heard the words stammer out.   *’No… We… I can’t’*  Her voice was soft as she spoke.   It felt to the Mandalorian that she didn’t want to hurt him.    He heard her apologize.  The regret in her voice was obvious.    He let her fingers slip from his as she stepped back towards her room still facing him.  


He gave her a slight smile, his eyes wide not hiding anything from her.   He found her incredibly attractive.   The sensations he felt at her touch were still tingling along his skin.  **”It’s okay Rin.”**  He said softly as he shifted to his right and let his shoulder lean against the wall.   **”There's no reason to apologize.  I… Shouldn’t have…”**  He said with a level of compassion that surprised even his young age.   He took a step back standing up straight.   The distance between them, slowly growing.

The young warrior moved and sat upon the edge of his bed and let out a long breath.  The feeling of the tingling sensation still forefront in his mind.  It was going to be a long night.

## **yogi_001** (02/05/2024 00:54:27) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1203866194327765062"></a>*1203866194327765062*

His sleep was troubled and dream filled.   Images floated by in his dream filled sleep.   Jedi and Mandalorian masters pushing an unknown Mandalorian in familiar armor onto his limits.  The images faded away as he finally drifted off into a deep slumber.   


His deep sleep continued on despite the quiet rumblings from the outer room.  At what sounded like a door closing Wes awoke, his blaster in hand.  The cobwebs of sleep quickly dissipated as he looked around his room.   His chrono said 08:35.  It was late.   Still wearing the bodysuit he had on when he laid down he quietly moved to the door.   Opening it slowly he looked around.  His blaster moved where his eyes did.   


**”Rin.”**  He called out as he moved to her door.   Opening it quietly he saw her bed was empty.   It looked neat but still slept in as if she just tossed the cover back over the bed.   Sweeping the rest of the apartment there was no sign of the woman he had just only met yesterday.   No sign of the permit she had gotten for him either.  


**”Stang”**  He swore aloud.   He made a mistake last night.  Yet he could still remember the feelings of electricity that danced across his skin from where they had touched.    


He took a deep breath as he fought to get his feelings under control.  He did what was comfortable for him.   Soon he had his armor on.  His helmet now hid his face from any observation that could be had.  He just hoped that he hadn’t ruined what working relationship with Rin he might have had.  


Despite looking around there was nothing that he could use to contact her.   They hadn’t traded com codes.    Letting out a sigh he went to the only place he thought he might find her.    


Wes pushed his way in through the cantina doors.   Looking around he saw no sign of Rin but he did see the same bartender from yesterday.    Walking up to the bar he waved the bartender down.    **”Have you seen Rin?”**

## **aliciagd** (02/05/2024 02:32:09) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1203890780708675664"></a>*1203890780708675664*

There's a larger quantity of non natives in the cantina in the morning. Most of them seeming to come here for breakfast before going about their day. The majority of them have the black armbands while a smaller number have a black and red arm band which hadn't been as noticeable the evening before. Wes realizes only those with the red and black armbands are carrying weapons.
The bartender eyes Wes warily as he continues cleaning. “**Rin said you might show up… She's in the back with the matron,**” he nods towards the door heading towards the employee area.
Walking down the short corridor, Wes can hear the distinct voices of two women talking around the din of metal scrapping on metal.  “**We worry about you… what was your father thinking; leaving you here all by yourself,**” an older woman’s voice pauses. “**This Drisk business you’ve involved yourself in…**”

Rin’s voice cuts her off. “**I appreciate your concern, but he has sent someone to help me.**”

“**Yes… Gren told me,**” the older woman's intones disapprovingly.

Just beyond a half door is a large kitchen used to prepare the establishment's dishes. Rin and an older Fakiri woman sit at a table off to the side of the door, out of the way of servers coming in and out. A pot of what looks like caf and a stack something similar to hotcakes is set aside, Rin apparently having already eaten her fill if the plate at her elbow is any indication.

## **yogi_001** (02/05/2024 03:49:06) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1203910146346975294"></a>*1203910146346975294*

Wes ignored the suspicious eyes from the bartender.  When he was told where Rin was he left the bartender without a second glance or thanks.   Quickly he walked towards the employee entrance to the kitchen area like he belonged there.   


Amid the din of the sounds of the working kitchen Wes began to pick up a conversation between one voice he recognized and one he didn’t.   Rin and another female were talking.  He slowed and stopped before he could be seen.   The woman was worried for her.   That Drisk was going to be a problem. One he was most likely going to have to deal with.  


Rin mentioned that someone has been sent to help her.   The disapproving tone from the other was evident.   Now more than ever the Mandalorian knew he was going to have to be vigilant to protect her.


He stepped up to the half door and took in the scene.   Caf and food were on the table.  His movement at the door was spotted as he saw Rin look his way.  Quickly she waved him in.  He watched as the Fakiri female stood and walked away but not before eyeing him as she moved off for a container.   


Wes stood near the table looking at Rin.   His helmet gave an unemotional face to the armored man before her.   He spoke calmly for only her to hear.   **”I can’t watch your back if I’m not with you Rin.”**  He paused.  **”What have you found out and do you have the permit you obtained for me.”**  


He had fallen back into his training despite the feelings that were now rolling around inside him since seeing Rin.   He had a job to do.   That had to be the priority.

Their journey takes them near the spaceport where a commercial district has been set up nearby allowing for easy access for imports. The warehouse the ‘Draays’ are utilizing for their front is by no means the largest of the warehouses in the area, but it seems of decent enough size for a merchant housing his goods. Again he underestimated her quickness.  With both hands he used his greater strength to push her away from him.  The farther away she was the less her quickness would be an advantage.

<a name="1204647665204338739"></a>*1204647665204338739*

He saw her hesitation as he offered a hand up.   After a quick second she took it.  Pulling gently he helped her to her feet.   She was rotating the pinned shoulder as she mentioned being out of practice.  


The laughter was in his eyes as well as his voice as he rubbed his left side.   His ribs were going to be bruised for a few days from the solid hit he took from the lithe woman.    **”Nonsense Rin.   You fought well against a larger and stronger opponent.  Whose only goal since he was young is to fight and win.   Training and fighting is all I do.”**  He waved his hand around to encompass the warehouse.  **”Stuff like this I haven’t the first clue on how to set up.   Strengths and weaknesses.   We all have them.  And we all learn from them too.””**   


He brought his hand to his side once again.  His smile remained as he rubbed his bruised ribs.   **”I have learned to be wary of that right you have and anyone who doesn’t take you seriously will be the one on the ground.   Not you.”**  


He saw her circling her shoulder and waved for her to come closer.  He watched as she took a cautious step towards him.   Removing the combat gloves he turned her around so her back was facing him.    Gently his hands took the shoulder he had used to pin her and slowly let his fingers work the muscles.   He wasn’t surprised at the strength he felt.   The bruise on his side that would be visible before long would be testament to her strength.  **”Here let me try and help this.  If you let it wait, the stiffness in the muscles later will be worse.”**  He said as he stood close.   His fingers rubbing the sore muscles of her shoulder.

<a name="1204759633986854943"></a>*1204759633986854943*

Rin warily lets him turn her till her back faced him. His proximity and the memory of the night before suddenly leaves her feeling rather exposed. As his hands begin working on her shoulder, she once again feels the tingles of electricity his strong, yet gentle touch brings. A small, pained moan escapes as he hits the sore muscles.

The Mandalorian wasn’t sure what was going on?   He wondered if he should mention it.

When she was out of sight in the upstairs area he focused on his thoughts and what was going through his head.    The tingles of electricity had faded to nothing again but the lingering effect was still forefront in his mind.  This was something new.  I was confusing yet he couldn’t find the word to describe it.   


What he did know.  He liked it.  He liked that he felt it from Rin.  


When Rin got close she could see that he was deep in thought.  His head looked down slightly and it looked as he was staring off into space.  


The movement of her sitting next to him caused him to come back from his thoughts.   He took the offered water as she asked about his ribs.   


**”Bruised, not broken.  I’ve had the luxury of knowing the difference between the two.”**  He said with a chuckle that made him wince slightly.   


He watched her activate the ice pack and hold it out while mentioning taking a look.  He nodded.  He lifted up his elbow and watched as she touched his skin with her fingers.  


Immediately the sensation was back like it had never stopped.  He looked up at her as she placed the ice pack gently to his side as her other hand was placed on his shoulder.  His body shuddered but he wasn’t sure if it was from the ice pack or the contact with Rin.   


He listened as she continued.  She didn’t agree with his assessment of himself.

## **yogi_001** (02/08/2024 12:03:50) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1205121815375118336"></a>*1205121815375118336*

Wes sat unmoving.   Fearing that his body would betray him and reach out to her.   In an effort to keep his free hand occupied he slipped it under his leg. It was an effort to trap it.   


It had taken a moment for her to talk.   He figured she was trying to figure out how to say what she did or didn’t know.   Her voice was soft and low as she started mentioning a connection between them.  Their proximity strengthening the connection.   


His head tilted slightly to the side when she paused.   His eyes searched hers for more explanation. He took a breath to say something but stopped when she started again.  What she said was unbelievable at first.  What she said he had seen first hand.   Working with Jedi off and on during the war the Mandalorian has seen some unexplainable happenings when it came to them.   **”Doesn't make sense.”**  He said softly but his words didn’t  have much conviction.  He did believe her.  


It wasn’t the same though.  He wasn’t a youngling as he had heard the young Jedi children called.  He was too old.   


He looked away for a second.   Then it hit him.   His head turned quickly to Rin.  **”A connection through the Force, with you?  You’re a…”**  He stopped thinking back.   He shook his head.  With his interactions among the Jedi he had never felt the sensation he recently had with Rin.   


He shifted his body weight and brought one leg up on to the crate it lay bent in between them.  The movement caused him to wince slightly but it took some pressure off his ribs.  


**”I’ve had interactions with Jedi on and off the battlefield where I’ve had to touch them and vice versa.   I’ve never felt, and I don’t even know if you know what I’m talking about, this charge when I touch you.”**  The last part was said with a bit of exasperation.  


His mouth closed as the proverbial wheels in his head started turning.

## **aliciagd** (02/09/2024 03:43:53) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1205358383885189251"></a>*1205358383885189251*

When the pearl reaches Wes, she lets her hand fall to rest on her knees in a relaxed, yet practiced position.  “**You'll want to be comfortable as you will be sitting like this for a while,**” she cautions. She waits for a moment to make sure he is actually going to hold his current position. 

“**There are such items which are imbued with such a purpose,  but no… nothing like that. Call it a challenge to figure out what it is.**  

“**Now… close your eyes,**” Rin says softly. 
“**The pearl in your hand has been attuned in the Force with a singular purpose.**” Her voice is low as she speaks, the sound of it carrying just enough for Wes to hear. “**As you breathe, focus on the pearl itself.**” She lets her voice trail off leaving Wes in silence.

The pearl feels strangely heavy in his hand for its size and on closer inspection seems to shift in color from pink to purple with a life of its own. Focusing on it, he can feel the energy contained within and realizes that energy is pulsing. While steady it takes on the reassuring cadence of a heartbeat. Moving deeper into the current, Wes starts getting impressions; the most prominent is a sleeping infant girl whose heart beats in time with the pearl. 

A gentle touch would bring Wes back to himself and when he's finally able to open his eyes, Rin is leaning close to him as she had reached over to shake his arm. A look of veiled concern meets his gaze.

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (02/09/2024 05:11:10) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1205380348800802866"></a>*1205380348800802866*

Wes nodded as he tried to get comfortable seated there in front of Rin.   He contemplated laying down on the hard duracrete.   After a moment he relaxed enough to where if he didn’t move too much or breath too deep the pain along his ribs was a large, dull ache.   He was beginning to believe he had a cracked rib or two.


**”I’m okay.”**   He half smiled and closed his eyes like she said.  Her voice was soft.  He focused upon it.   Soon he was focused upon the pearl as her voice trailed off into nothing.   


It was quiet.   Like the haunting quiet on the battlefield when the fighting was over.   The absence of sound was deafening to the Mandalorian.   The only thing he could see and or sense was the pearl.  It felt heavier than it should have been as the color of it shifted from pink to purple.  There was no pattern to it.  Colors shifted on their one as if it was alive. 


He focused on it.  Narrowed his senses until it was the only thing.   He felt the beat emanating from it.  A pulse, steadily beating like a heart beat.  The warrior fell in step with the measured beats.  Slipping in deeper as time passed.  Time may have stopped, he wasn't sure.  


The image of a tiny infant girl appeared.   Sleeping peacefully as her heart beat in unison with the pearl.  He reached out to touch her.   Just as his hand was about to gently touch her she was gone.  He felt a gentle touch and a presence.   It was close.  Very close but he felt no threat from it.   Finally he was able to open his eyes.   Rin was close.   Very close as he felt her hand shaking his arm.  The same feeling as before when they had touched had returned.  The only thing he saw was a look of deep concern.   


**”The little girl.   Rin, did you see the little girl?”**  His voice was a whisper as he leaned slowly towards her unsteady.

Anyone who sees you like that might think you’re dead.**” Her look of concern has now been replaced with one of curiosity. “**With some time, you’ll be able to control how deep you go so you don’t lose awareness of your surroundings, it can even be heightened, and then your body can respond much more quickly.**”

Wes took in what she had said.  Apparently he was deep in his meditation.  When she said several hours he raised an eyebrow as it only seemed like a few moments.  If he was alone he was going to have to make sure that he was more careful about where, when and with whom he did that again.  


He felt it as removed her hand from his arm.   The reassuring electrified tingle he had associated with her touch started to fade.  He closed his eyes as the feeling subsided into nothing yet the memory remained.  **”Does this mean we’ll be working together for a period of time”** He asked after she cautioned him from doing it again without her around.

Thank you”**  Without thinking and to show appreciation he reached up with his right hand and laid it upon her shoulder. **”I’m sorry.”** He said as he slowly stood taking care about his side that was feeling better.

I hope it’s only that.”**  He said as he reached for an armor piece.   **”I’m not sure I can handle another type of connection through the Force right now.”**  He said it as a matter of fact despite his smile.   He was in unknown territory.   The connection and attraction to Rin was strong and it  felt like it was getting stronger.   He knew she felt it as well.

Rin doesn't need to be told twice as she gracefully jumps down from the bar seat and heads for the exit. Familiar with the route, she ends up taking a shortcut away from the main path and directly to the alley of the apartment building. The way had grown cramped for a portion of it, not allowing the pair to walk side by side. 

Punching in the door code, Rin heads into the apartment and stops short just a few steps from the door. With a short motion so indicates to Wes to not say anything, while her eyes scan for the trouble she is sensing. Nothing looks outwardly out of place and the apartment is empty, but something was still nagging her. 

With her fingers outstretched, she stalks about the apartment. She stops as she reaches the table where the various parts had been left scattered about. Picking up one in particular she turns it in her hands, the same assessing look she had given both the datacard and Wes's armor playing on her face. Slowly, she sets the part back down and turns to face Wes.  She points to the part and then to her ear.

“**It's still nice outside, why don't we eat in the courtyard,**” she says casually.

As Rin looked around the apartment Wes stood just inside the door and slowly closed it.  And looked around from his vantage point.  A quick moment later she set a part down indicating something was wrong.   Perhaps a bug.   With her suggestion to eat outside.   He nodded.  


**”That's what I said on the way back here.  Enjoy it while we can right?”**  He turned and opened the door.  Stepping out to the hall with eyes alert.  Casually he shifted the bag to his left hand thus freeing his right for his weapon.  He led the way down nthe hall away from the apartment.

## **aliciagd** (02/13/2024 15:52:48) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1206991373425840158"></a>*1206991373425840158*

Rin watches with a neutral expression as Wes finalizes his preparations and his own demeanor changes. A small smile breaks through as he reminds her to watch her back. “**Good luck,**” she says at last as he walks out the door.

----

At the predetermined location a speeder is waiting for Wes with a familiar pair of B1 battle droids accompanying it. With no other sign of occupants it seems it was sent to transport Wes alone. One of the droids spots Wes and in confirmation one points to the speeder. “**You’re to come with us,**” it says, personal skills not really this model of droid’s forte.

The speeder takes off as soon as the droids get into the speeder. Proceeding through the main road of the city it eventually arrives at the outskirts where a large walled building has been designated as the Separatist headquarters on the planet, or has Rin had been referring to as the Annex. As the gates open to allow the speeder through, the nickname seems to make sense as a town of its own springs up before Wes. The Annex seems to function through the use of droids, of which any living sentients are few and have the look of mercenaries confirmed by the red and black armbands indicating they’ve been allowed to bear arms outside of the Annex. Eventually the speeder stops in front of the more prominent central buildings where a protocol droid awaits at the top of a series of stairs.

“**Greetings, his excellency, Ambassador Kolak Invat is expecting you.**” Waiting for Wes to show signs he is going to follow, it proceeds to lead him into the building to the central lift where the top floor is selected.

Non-droid population was very low.   All that he saw were others wearing the same black and red armband that he also sported.   


When the speeded finally stopped Wes looked to his right and was greeted by the Ambassadors protocol droid.    Like most of its kind it looked and acted flighty.   It seemed to be waiting impatiently.  


Wes removed himself from the speeder and walked up the steps not answering the droid.   When it took the hint that he was ready to follow it finally started to lead him into the building and finally the central lift.    A moment later the lift doors opened up.  

Wes when the droid didn’t move right away Wes glanced sidelong at it.  It seemed to startle the droid and it  proceeded out followed by the Mandalorian.   Looking around Wes took in the surroundings of the penthouse.

Now they were just going to need a speeder.    **”Renting a speeder won’t be a problem.  I was also given a credit chip.   So that’s covered.”**  He took another bit.   As he considered the two chips.   


**”Is the apartment going to be a safe place to check these out?”**  He avoided using any terminology Rin used to describe her ability to sense the objects.  He wasn’t sure if she took care of the bugs or if there would even be more there waiting for them.

Wes sat upon the log.   They both sat quietly contemplating whatever came to mind.  Wes was trying to practice being calm.   It wasn’t much different than what he always did before his newly discovered affinity to the Force.    It was common for him to quiet himself before battle.  Now he knew why or at least had an idea why he did.   


He also practiced by reaching out to Rin.   It seemed easier when he did so with her than if he just bluntly reached out.    Her assumption was that it was due to the bond that had formed between them.  They could easily reach out to one another.   


Stretching her legs she deposited the ration containers they had recently used.  When she came back she was holding something.  Explaining what it was as she sat back down.   


The idea was foreign to him.   Using the Force to open it.  **”I have no idea how to do that.”**  He said as he took it from her and held it in the glass of his palm.   Moving his wrist and his head he looked it over.   **”How does it impart its knowledge?   Wait.   Let’s not put the Bantha before the cart.  First, how do I access it?”**

Getting comfortable on the log, Rin pulls her jacket close against the cooling night air. “**Focus on it and reach out to it with the Force.**” She goes back to her stargazing while she leaves Wes to figure it out, not wanting to pressure him by looking over his shoulder. 

The crystalline cube begins to glow as Wes reaches out to it with the Force, the corners turning as it activates and hovers slightly above the palm of his hand. Rin gives him a smile before her focus comes back to the cube. A hologram of a middle aged Twi’lek appears, hovering above the activated cube.

## **yogi_001** (02/19/2024 17:14:23) <br style='clear: both;'>

Figuratively he took a step back and approached it as if he was reaching out to Rin.  The bond they shared made it easier and it continued to become easier the more they interacted that way.   


Slowly a small glow started at the corners and then permeated it way through the box.  He watched in amazement as the corners turned and it lifted off his hand.   He had just done something he never thought possible.  Elation could be felt radiating off of him.

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (02/20/2024 02:01:30) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1209318884323106887"></a>*1209318884323106887*

Rin eyes the coin reticently as it's placed in the palm of her hand and fights off the impressions she senses from it. Instead she focuses on Wes's words. While he gave her the coin and the promise out of love, there was to her an underlying sense in doom. If the time ever came where she would need the protection of the Mandalorian clans, then she would no longer be part of the Order and  cast out to make her own way. 

Pushing the thoughts to the side, she leans toward him to seal their unsaid promises with a kiss. She lets his emotions wash over her and mingle with her own till they are once more one. 

It's only the chill that brings her back to herself and is reminded how exposed they are. With a shiver she draws back reluctantly. “**Maybe we should turn in?**” she suggests, eying the small tent they had erected.

## **yogi_001** (02/20/2024 02:41:20) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1209328910135857182"></a>*1209328910135857182*

The kiss they shared let their emotions mingle and become one with each other.  They broke the kiss and Wes simply enjoyed being close to Rin.   Despite being out in the colder evening air and under the stars this was where he wanted to be.   With Rin.   When she mentioned turning in he nodded but held her up before they entered the tent.   


**”I’m not sure what we’re going to run into down there.  Are you armed?   I guess what I’m asking is do you have your Jedi weapon?”**

It resonated as if it was alive.    Rin talked about master Ven and the battle at Geonosis.   He noticed that there was no activation switch.

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (02/20/2024 20:27:51) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1209597306165526630"></a>*1209597306165526630*

Rin nods and waits for Wes to settle in before turning the lantern off, throwing the tent into blackness. Wes’s sleep is filled with strange dreams he can’t seem to grasp onto. During one moment of partial wakefulness one comes to him, but it doesn’t have the sense of a dream. Crouched at the edge of a cliff, the sheer drop reveals a large basin where a nearby waterfall runs its course. There’s a low growl from behind, the only warning before the lupine creature leaps from the shadows and charges. Only quick reflexes prevent the lupines maw from catching hold. There’s a moment of hesitation allowing the creature to regroup and try again, this time however, with a single step the vision leaps off the cliff, angling for the basin below. Youthfulness and the thrill overwrite any sense of danger before the crash into the water knocks all breath out. *Why did you jump?* a voice asks evenly with an underlying curiosity. The dream ends without an answer. 

The night passes without interruption and before dawn Rin leaves the tent quietly attempting not to bother Wes with her departure. She finds a spot at the edge of the cliff to sit and look out over the canyon as the sun starts to rise.

Grabbing two ration packs from the speeder he walked over to where Rin sat at the edge of the cliff.   The cliff face reminded him of the dream he just had.

Unbalanced by the pack, she reaches out desperately to catch herself as she begins to fall. Reflexively, Wes reaches out and nearly loses his own balance, barely managing to keep hold of the wall. Several feet down, Wes can see Rin has managed to stop her plummet on a slim outcropping, but at the moment she seems to be stuck in place. 

“**I’m fine,**” she calls up to him in an attempt to assuage his concern. Looking around she attempts to shift her foot, causing pieces of the wall around her to crumple under foot. “**I can’t see a way down from here.**” Not able to get down, she starts looking to see if she can head up the wall.

With his armor he figured he was almost, if not more, twice her weight.   Satisfied that the rope was as secure as it was going to get he yelled down.  **”Alright Rin. **”Oof!”** Wes felt like the wind had been knocked from him.  His eyes registered and he was scant feet above the ground.  He could see and hear rocks hitting the ground around him.    A second later he hit the ground.    Thankfully his arms were already out and helped break his fall.   


With a pained grunt he rolled over as quickly as he could only to see Rin falling towards him.  From that height she was going to be hurt especially the way she was uncontrollably coming down.   Knowing he couldn’t get up quick enough to catch her he closed his eyes and reached out through the bond they shared.   With his arms up raised he tried to stop her.  


He felt something between them, he wasn’t sure if it was the air, but he was pushing up from his body towards Rin.  He saw her through the Force.   Yet seeing wasn’t exactly accurate.   Her presence above him was coming closer.   He wasn’t sure what he was doing other than trying to simply hold her and keep her from crashing into the ground by pushing outward towards her. 



He then heard her say his name from the ground beside him.   It sounded far away. Looking to his left he opened his eyes, his sight and hearing came back into focus.  He saw her laying on her back next to him an arms length away.   As he let his arm fall towards her and grabbed her hand.  The contact brought the familiar sensation he had come to know from her touch.

## **yogi_001** (02/22/2024 19:00:27) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1210300088665243688"></a>*1210300088665243688*

He gave her a smirk at the sarcastic comment.  **”At least that hasn’t been injured.”**  He tried to say lightheartedly but the chuckle caused him to wince slightly.    


He removed the gauze from the head wound.  It wasn’t deep but she was right about head wounds.  **”Yeah it’s not too deep of a cut.”**  He quickly put the gauze back in place and applied some pressure despite the wince of pain he saw on her face.  


They were both quiet for a moment.   Wes used that time to look around to see where they were.   Looking up he realized they were a good forty meters down from where the ledge gave way.    They were lucky.   


He heard her question about using the Force to stop her.   He looked back down at her.  Removing his helmet, his face was blank.   With a small shrug he simply looked at her.  **”I don’t really know.    I knew I needed to stop you from falling.  I reached out to you with our bond.  I’m not sure what I did.   I just tried to catch you or push you up.  Maybe a combination of both.  I’m just glad I didn’t hurt you more.”**

She frowns as she looks up to where they had fallen, realizing how badly things could have been. “**We’re going to need to find a better way to get back. It will be difficult by ourselves, but with the Fakiri?**” Then looking at where they have yet to go. “**I think we know now why the Ambassador wasn’t going to risk his own men on this hunt, huh?**”

## **aliciagd** (02/23/2024 02:33:36) <br style='clear: both;'>

Rin watches at first annoyed and then passively as Wes rummages through her pack to reconsolidate the load. Finishing the rest of the ration, she takes a drink of the water before tossing it into her pack.  He had told her to take it slow, and as she starts to stand quickly realizes he was right. Meeting Wes's gaze she looks up once more the way they had come. “**We're partners,**” she says simply to his gratitude.  She had done what she had to at the time to protect him. 

Now that she's standing and upright,  she doesn't find it too difficult to stay so. Slowly she makes her way over the river's edge and bending down she rinses off her blood from her hands and face the best she can. The cold water sends an invigorating jolt through her. 

Feeling much better she collects her pack and moves to stand next to Wes, taking his hand for a reassuring squeeze.  “**Let's see how far we can get.  Maybe keep an eye open for a cave or somewhere to camp if not the way across.**”

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (02/23/2024 15:50:00) <br style='clear: both;'>

Rin returns his smile, and gives his hand another squeeze. She lets go for a moment only to shift her pack to a more comfortable position for the long walk. “**A fire would be nice…**” she comments idly as they start their walk up the bank. Her focus turns to their path ahead.

It was fortunate the way was easy enough as at times her vision blurred and she relied more on her Force imbued senses and her contact with Wes to keep from losing her way or stumbling. She quickly loses track for how long they walk in her effort to keep pace.

It’s with relief when Wes spots the cave up ahead for them to settle in for the night. Set up into the cliff face it requires a small climb which she manages with Wes’s help. Unslinging the pack, she lets it fall heavily to the ground and she resists the urge to collapse alongside it. Instead she starts the methodical process of helping to set up their campsite. “**I didn’t see anything suitable for burning,**” Rin comments as she lays out her sleeping bag.

I know you don’t agree with it, but I’ll accept that you at least understand.**” Lifting her head, she turns to look up at him and gives him a small smile. “**Until the time comes… I plan to enjoy these moments.**” 
Her head resumes its earlier placement on his shoulder as she considers the day’s events. “**Yes… the cliff,**” she says quietly and her earlier mood returns for a moment before she manages to cover it up. “**This wasn’t the first time I’ve fallen, you’d think I’d learn to take better care,**” she says trying to be good natured about her self critique.

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (02/25/2024 15:16:08) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1211330802504437760"></a>*1211330802504437760*

**”Yes, enjoying the moments.  We never know when it will end.”**  He gave her hand a firm squeeze.  **”As far as the cliff, that’s just a roll of the sabacc dice.   Sometimes luck runs out.  When that happens it’s good to have people around you that you can trust your life with.”** 


He reached for another log and placed it on the fire.   **”If we manage it carefully it may last most of the evening.  I’d suggest staying close tonight while we rest.”** 


He sat quietly with her for a moment.  **”I’ll try to keep my emotions under better control.  I don’t know if it’s the Force or the bond but I can feel them from you as well.  I’ve never been this wide open to anyone.  This is new to me.  So much is new to me right now.”**

## **aliciagd** (02/26/2024 00:27:10) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1211469474977550396"></a>*1211469474977550396*

Rin readily agrees to take him through the altered forms in the morning. Sitting across from him she takes his hands in hers.  The first time he had meditated she had avoided contact with him and hadn't been able to guide him. Now, they could use their bond to his advantage.
“**I'll just help you not go into a deep trance like you did the first time. When done correctly you're still aware of your surroundings and you'll be able to come out when you need to and feel more rested than when sleeping.**”
With a squeeze, she walks him through the basics of entering the meditative trance. Soon enough he finds his way into the trance and she nudges him from going too far. Gently, she let go of his hands and leaves them resting on his knees. 
She banks the coals for the morning as the last remnant of the fire begins to die off. . Wrapping the blanket around her shoulders against the growing chill, she glances over at Wes as she decides to resume her own meditation.

Towards dawn, Rin leaves the cave in search of more wood and returns with enough to restart the fire for heating up more food and water. She waits for Wes to come out of the trance on his own, a hot drink waiting for him.

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

Her calming voice along with nudges through their bond helped him relax and fall into the trance.   At one point he felt her pull him back a bit.   Slowly he settled into place.  Her calm voice guided him there.  


He sat there still aware of what was going on around him.   The fire had died down and he could hear Rin’s slowed breath.   It sounded like she had gone back to meditating.   Though this time it wasn’t a deeper trance.   She was in a state like his.  


He felt and heard her moving next to him.  He felt no alarm so he continued to stay in the trance.  Sometime later he felt warmth radiating towards him.  Wes felt like he might have gone a bit deeper into his meditation when Rin moved away.  Thankfully the warmth from the fire drew him back.   From there he decided to end the trance and open his eyes.    His breathing quickened as he shrugged his shoulders and the smell of food tickled his nose.

Finally, they escape the current and set foot on the bank. Thoroughly wet from the waist down. Rin sits in the bank and starts taking her boots and socks off. Letting her feet dry out, she takes a look at her lightsaber to make sure it hadn't been damaged. Satisfied she returns it to its place and pulls out her leftover rations to snack on. “**Well other than being thoroughly wet now… that went well.**”

Not wanting to be in the dark cave any longer, she heads for the cave mouth and finds a place in the early evening sun to sit. 
She takes off her pack and adjusts herself on the ground to be more comfortable.  “**Our bond seems to make it easier to do such things. I know you do it to help me, but still... you must be careful.**” The concern is evident in her tone. 
For the moment she decides not to discuss the artifact. “**Do you think it's safe to stay here tonight or should we find somewhere else? We also need to decide what to do from here, what with the Fakiri dead.**”

## **yogi_001** (03/05/2024 11:54:19) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1214541501665771550"></a>*1214541501665771550*

The confused look on his face probably said it all when she said that he had shared some of his energy with her.  Was such a thing even possible?  He had let go of her hands after she had stood.  She made her way closer to the mouth of the cave and the sun that waited there.   After she took a few steps he bent down retrieving the artifact, glow rod and his helmet. I don’t know.   This is all happening quickly.”**  A level of frustration entered his voice.  **”I don’t want to hurt you.   I’ll do my best to reign it in.”**  


He grabbed a food packet from his pack and sat quietly gathering himself, trying to bring a sense of calm like she had taught him only days before. 


Days.


They both sat quietly.  Wes realized that his training was somewhat linear before.  Now it was…not and also complicated.  He could hurt himself and others now without realizing it.  He looked at Rin as she sat quietly.  He figured she was trying to put pieces together about the artifact.  She finally broke the silence and ask about the steps forward.

There's no response from Rin as Wes calls her name. Her breathing and heartbeat have slowed, indicative of a trance. The only thing unusual is the now pulsing cut kyber which has seemingly come to life in her hands. Her fingers clench around the artifact almost reflexively, her grip on it now unyielding.

This happens a few times, each time the crystal growing dimmer until finally it's extinguished.  Her fingers spasm, but refuse to open to relinquish the gem. ## **yogi_001** (03/07/2024 14:19:31) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1215302821705027614"></a>*1215302821705027614*

Time passes agonizingly slow.   He watched what seemed to be a battle between Rin and the crystal.  More than once he reached for her hand and stopped remembering his pledge to her.    Test as time dragged on he was becoming increasingly more worried.  This seems completely different from the times before.   


Despite his complete lack of training even he could feel that something was wrong.  He didn’t know what to do.  For the first time in his life, he felt helpless.  


**”Rin!   Fight it!   Break the connection.  Come back to me.  Use my voice.   Use the bond we share.”**  His own breath was coming quickly as his frustration increased.  


Standing he thought about simply grabbing her hand and prying her fingers open but he gave her his word.  


**”Kriff it!”** He swore.  Frustrated, he knelt down again to both knees and sat back to his heels.  He tried to calm himself.  He placed his hand over hers, careful to not touch her or the artifact.   He closed his eyes and tried to calm himself.  **”Rin.”**  He said aloud.  As he spoke he tried to force his presence to her.   Give her something to latch on to.  His anxiety rose and he knew he was failing.   


He took a breath and focused like he did before a battle.   He was always able to find that calmness then.   This was a battle and he needed to treat it as such.   He felt his pulse and breath slow as he calmed himself.   His senses became more acute.   He could hear water dripping somewhere off deeper in the cave.  


*’Rin’*  He thought.   He pushed his words out to her  *’Fight it.  Release the crystal, turn your hand over.’*.  He could feel her through the Bond.  The struggle she was going through.   The pull that the crystal was having on her.   He drew deep within himself.  *’Drop it Cyra’ika! Now!’*  He shouted in his mind.

## **aliciagd** (03/07/2024 17:16:56) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1215347467139158016"></a>*1215347467139158016*

Rin’s fingers spasm once again as Wes reaches out to her through the Force and through his urging her hand does finally open. The artifact slips through her fingers to land between them with a sharp clink as it hits the stone floor. She’s then still, her breathing heavy and erratic fighting back more sobs. Her training and still irrational mind war with each other. 

Eventually her training wins out and she’s finally able to look at Wes. Still obviously shaken by the experience, Rin is slowly regaining her usual decorum now that she’s no longer being influenced by the artifact. “**I could hear you… reaching out to me.**” she says at last, her voice unsteady.

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (03/07/2024 20:25:29) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1215394919443857498"></a>*1215394919443857498*

Wes watched as her fingers moved.  If he could have willed her to drop the crystal he would have.  All he could do was urge her to action.  


As soon as he saw it slip through her fingers he felt her come back and he felt what he could only describe as anguish.  The shock of the experience suddenly took hold of Rin as she fought the demons she just encountered. 


As she started sobbing into her hands he edged closer and laid a hand on her shoulder.  He was careful to not do what he did earlier but the tingle of their bond flared to life at the contact.  


He knelt beside her as if standing guard until she was able to compose herself.   Finally he felt her take a deep breath and let it out slowly.    Despite the calming technique she was still shaken up from the experience.  **”I’m here Rin.  Take your time.”**  He said quietly.  Reassuring her that she was safe.  


A moment later she was looking at him.  Her eyes were wet with tears.  Her voice was shaky as she said she could hear him.   


He smiled as his own eyes became wet.  He wasn’t even sure what he did or if it would work.  His other hand came up and took hers that held the crystal.  


He smiled and tried to joke.  **”You’re not getting rid of me that easily.”**  He gave her hand a squeeze and then quickly let it go.   Leaning to his side he grabbed her tea that had cooled considerably.  **”Here.   Drink this and I’ll get some water.”**

It will fight back, but we must persevere.**” There was no doubt in her mind they would succeed, to do so would be to fail before having begun. “**I'll protect you from its influence the best I can, but I expect it will discover our bond and try to use it. **” 
Knowing he still questioned what she expected from him she gave his gloved hand a squeeze. “**You'll need to lend me your strength at times and just be here. I'll be able to use our bond to stay centered.**”

---

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (03/11/2024 16:27:02) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1216784460352196639"></a>*1216784460352196639*

Wes sat down across from Rin.  She took the artifact from his hand and took it with her free hand.   They touched at three points. Their knees and the hand they each held.  Wes figured that was for the purpose of sharing his strength with her.  It made sense as their touch induced a physical reaction to the contact they shared.  He was ready to help and support her effort to clean the crystal so to speak.   She was the tip of the spear.  He was ready to make sure she stayed sharp and focused.  Deadly.  His demeanor and emotions reflected as such. 


She explained once more that the essence may come for him as well when it sensed the bond between them.   He gave her a nod and a reassuring squeeze of her hand.  


This was going to be a battle like none he’s never seen or participated in.  Yet he treated it like any other, an absence of fear.   By his side was a woman he trusted.  A woman he had opened himself up to.   A woman he had fallen for.  He didn’t hide it as right now there was no hiding anything from her.   


**”I'm with you Rin.  When you need me I will be here.  My strength and my will will be lent to you.”**

---

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (03/12/2024 01:44:51) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1216924840746025080"></a>*1216924840746025080*

Rin gives Wes a nod before she closes her eyes. Her grasp on his hand grows lighter as she enters her meditation, her breathing imperceptible the deeper she goes. At first she doesn’t reach out to the artifact, but when she does it comes to life in her hands once more, pulsing red in her hand.

For the first time, through Rin, Wes gets a sense of the living crystal. Rage, hate, pain and fear had been poured into the crystal until it had been corrupted away from its natural affinity and been forced to embody the essence of its former master.
It’s this essence Rin begins to cajole, urging it to share with her its history. At first it seems all too eager to in an attempt to shock her and wear her down. She urges it on, and the essence seems to grow stronger with each passing moment as it revels in the hatred which has consumed it.
A wave of the dark emotions wash over her, and Wes feels her sway beneath the onslaught.  It's then the dark presence detects Wes and the whispers begin to invade his thoughts. They start as indecipherable murmurs but then suddenly become unbearably loud. 

For a moment Wes is dazed and disoriented. When he regains his senses he's no longer in the cave. The morning sun is filtering through the curtains and falls on the face of Rin laying beside him. It's not Rin's apartment on Fakir, but somewhere new. As he shifts closer to her, his hand falls around her waist to rest on her very swollen belly.
