<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (03/12/2024 14:34:26) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1217118514515542046"></a>*1217118514515542046*

For the first time Wes may have truly experienced hate and rage.   He had an increased level of respect for Rin if this was a common occurrence when using her ability.  It felt as if the crystal was alive and that felt…dangerous.  


He squeezed her hand, at least he thought he did, to reassure her that he was her with her on this journey.  


He could feel the crystals hate rising as Rin tempted it.  Flaunted her calmness at it.  She seemed to be getting the desired effect as she drew out the essence of the stone.   It was then that Wes felt the despair and dark emotions ebb out from it.  He felt Rin slip some and he gave her his strength.   His ability in the Force was very limited but his will wasn’t.   He felt her resolve solidify with his help.  


Unfortunately his help didn’t not go unnoticed.  


Whispers suddenly became noticeable at the edge of his perception.  He worked at shutting them out but slowly they became louder.  An instant later it was as if he was in the middle of a loud battle with separatists and then quiet.  


The warm morning sun warmed his face and the songs of the birds outside tickled his ears.  Looking over he saw the beautiful face of Rin lying next to him, her face glowing in the sun.  He rolled to his side on the comfortable bed and wiggled closer.  The cold cave of Fakir this wasn’t but it still felt close as if the memory was still active in his mind.  


Hugging her he smiled.   His hand moved to rub her pregnant belly.  She carried their child. Their daughter.   **”Good morning Cyra’ika”**

## **yogi_001** (03/12/2024 17:11:54) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1217158140869742693"></a>*1217158140869742693*

He nodded as if remembering.  He looked back at his wife and smiled as finally put on her boots.  


**”Good.  It’s been too long.  Do you think he will be happy with the name we chose for his granddaughter?”**  He was happy his father was finally going to meet Rin.  A bit of sadness passed by at the thought of his mother not being here too.  


As he mentioned it he paused midstep.  His gaze encompassed a large mirror that adorned the wall over the antique dresser.   In the mirror the image caused his breath to catch.    The reflection he saw wasn’t the room he was in.   It was dark and light flickered as if from a campfire.  The strong acrid smell of smoke filled his senses.  Two people sat on the ground.  Knees touching and each held the hand of the other.    In the woman’s other upturned hand was a glowing red crystal.   


His eyes widened as he looked back at his wife who was putting on her robe.   She tied it gently around her full belly.   


Looking back to the mirror the image changed, their hands had gripped tighter and the woman’s head hung lower.   Wes felt a tugging at his senses.  The crackling fire.  The smell of the smoke.   The coolness of the air on his exposed skin.   


Fakir.  The cave.  **”Rin!”**  He said aloud, turning back to her as the image before him dissolved and was replaced by her sitting before him.  The crystal flaring in her hand.  


*”Noooo!”*  He yelled.   Not sure if it was even audible.   *”Rin it’s not real.  We’re in the cave!  It’s the crystal.”*  He focused on their bond and lent her more strength.   *”Fight it.  Use the bond, my strength.”*

## **aliciagd** (03/12/2024 19:06:46) <br style='clear: both;'>

Rin’s demeanor changes as Wes comes back to himself. Taking a different tact with the essence in the crystal she pulls together her own emotions, sharing with it memories in an effort to connect with it. The feel of dough between her small fingers combined with the smell of bread as a brown haired woman laughs across from her. The energy between them flares to life, their conjoined hands a conduit flowing to the red crystal. It brightens with a brilliance casting away all the shadows in the dark cave. All resistance from the crystal stops and as Rin draws back and opens her eyes to look down at the crystal in her hand, it glows with a pale white light.

Looking up at Wes, Rin gives him a small tired smile. “**It’s done.**”

He walked back to where Rin was finishing up what she was working on.  Looking up at the sky she heard him ask a question.  **”How long do we have?”**

---

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (03/30/2024 14:55:02) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1223646679216164925"></a>*1223646679216164925*

Rin nods with the decision and goes to collect a blanket from the Fakiri’s possessions to wrap him in it. As the finishes her task, her gaze follows Wes' to the sky outside the cave mouth. Already the sound of a ship's engine can be heard echoing through the canyon, growing louder as it draws closer. “**Not long enough,**” she says evenly, her practiced tone hiding her own thoughts. 

She doesn't dare to look at him as she steps out of the cave. They both have had to resort to their training to deal with the change. She had hoped their farewell would have been on their terms, but circumstances were now against them.

Stepping out into a small clearing, Rin activates a beacon on her bracer to direct the ship to their exact location. “**At least we won't have worry about the hike back,**” she quips lightly, watching as the ship takes up a position above them. The YT would be a common enough sight, if it wasn't for the fact someone had gone to pains to paint it red and white. While the ship holds steady above them, the ramp lowers and a line is thrown down from within. 

Rin assists Wes in hooking the body of the Fakiri to the line to be pulled up first and then watches with him as the body is hoisted up with the assistance of the winch. “**Whatever happens next…**” she starts, her piercing gaze meeting his, but her thought is interrupted as the line is thrown back down.

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (03/30/2024 16:00:19) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1223663108577558679"></a>*1223663108577558679*

**”As odd as it may sound, I was looking forward to the hike back.”**  His tone was neutral despite how he felt as he suppressed his feelings.  It was harder than he realized.  He didn’t have years of training like Rin did.  


He turned and looked at her.   It was a brief glance and he knew it was a mistake as he fought to control how he felt.   Turning away quickly he moved to the body and with her help they both secured the body to the line.  For a moment they watched it ascend to the ship.   


He looked at her again knowing that he shouldn’t.  He saw her piercing blue eyes as they penetrated to his core.  *’Whatever happens next…”*  She started but was cut off as the line was thrown back and hit the ground next to them.  He gave her a nod.   **”Know that we will always be with each other, no matter where we may go.”**  He finished as he grabbed the line and handed it to her.  **”Ni kar’taylir darassum gar.”**  He let some emotion enter his voice knowing that it wouldn’t be heard by anyone above.   He hoped she would understand what he said.  He wished he hadn’t waited to say it to her.    The whine of the ship's repulsors were loud enough to drown out his voice.   As quickly as he let the emotion into his voice he squashed it again.

## **yogi_001** (03/30/2024 16:00:48) <br style='clear: both;'>

He waited one last time for the line to drop for him.   Grabbing a hold of the line she secured it to himself as he looked around one last time.  A small smile appeared beneath his helmet as images of the night before flash quickly into his mind.    With a deep breath he pushed the memory away and gave the signal to be pulled up.  With a tug the winch attached to the line started and he was slowly lifted from the ground.   His body twirled slowly as he looked around taking in the sight of the canyons and the land from the increasing height.   The deep blue sky reminded him of her eyes.

Mandalorian translation 

Ni kar’taylir darassum gar.  -  I love you.

## **yogi_001** (04/02/2024 01:12:24) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1224526821618352148"></a>*1224526821618352148*

Thirty minutes in, Wes decided to practice something Rin had taught him.  He closes his eye for a moment as he hooked his thumbs into his utility belt.  He took a deep breath.  Since Rin had started her debrief he had been anything but calm.   Since they had decided to be open and honest for the debrief all that they had discovered about him was going to come out.   He needed to be focused and ready.  


Standing and alert he entered a light meditative trance while still alert to his immediate surroundings.  He heard the office door open.   A moment later he heard the Jedi's voice calling his name.  Opening his eyes he reached for his helmet and was soon walking up the stairs.  


Upon entering he saw that Silas had taken his seat again at the table.  Looking to his right he saw Rin sitting on the floor.   She had taken the same position he had seen several times since he had met her.   He could see the calm rise and fall of her chest and he knew she was meditating.  His gaze lingered for only a second or two before he took a seat opposite Silas and set his helmet to his left.   


Silas started right with the last event and the corrupted kyber crystal that Rin had purified with his help.  Wes retrieved the box that contained the crystal from the secure pouch on his utility belt.  He turned the box over with his fingers and set it on the table.  Leaning forward he slid it towards Silas.  **”Here it is.”**

---

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (04/02/2024 16:41:09) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1224760548533731498"></a>*1224760548533731498*

With a small nod Silas reaches out the short distance to open the box and reveal the artifact. He looks it over for a moment from where it rests before turning his attention to Wes. “**It was quite reckless of the two of you to attempt this,**” he says evenly, indicating the crystal. “**The consequences could have been fatal.**” He holds up a hand to waylay any sort of objection. “**I would be remiss in my duty as her mentor and my part in your own awakening if I didn’t give some sort of reprimand. Many Jedi, in their hubris, have attempted what you both did and not survived.**” He pauses as he looks between Wes, Rin and the artifact. “**Under the circumstances, I understand why the risk was taken.**” 

Reaching out he takes the artifact in hand and looks it over, inspecting the kyber crystal carefully. He turns to where Rin is sitting and calls for her. She stands gracefully and comes to stand next to Silas as he holds out the artifact for her take. Like in the cave, it begins to glow as it responds to her touch. He nods confirming something to himself before holding his hand out to take the crystal back. With a small gesture, Rin is dismissed once more. She gives Wes a small wink in reassurance as she turns to resume her early meditation.

Silas returns the artifact to the box and closes it with a snap. “**Your plan is to return this to the ambassador?**”

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (04/02/2024 18:41:59) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1224790956507660339"></a>*1224790956507660339*

Wes sat and listened quietly as Silas sternly yet quietly admonished him and Rin for the risk they took.  He followed it up with an understanding of the situation.     


He wasn’t intending to speak but he found himself doing so.  **”Yes, it was dangerous.  I saw something of myself that I didn’t even know was within me.  It showed me what I desired.   Something I didn’t even know I wanted.  It tried to lure me.   Lure the two of us and we resisted its temptations.”**   He let the breath out that he found himself to be holding. 


**”We trusted each other.”**  He said with confidence as he let his gaze shift to her for a second before looking back at The Jedi.   Wes fought to control his emotions but he felt like no matter what he did, thought or felt the experienced Jedi Master would sense it.  Still he did his best to somewhat keep it under control.  


He nodded in response to his question about the case.  **”Yes, that's my intent.  The presence that was within it is no longer there.   The ability it possessed to hurt someone is now gone.  I need to return it and the Fakiri to the Ambassador.”**  He paused for a second.  “**To not return it would bring dishonor upon me and my Clan.”**

## **aliciagd** (04/03/2024 09:07:10) <br style='clear: both;'>

## **aliciagd** (04/07/2024 18:22:45) <br style='clear: both;'>

## **aliciagd** (04/26/2024 01:22:59) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1233226792102396004"></a>*1233226792102396004*

Veva doesn't miss a beat as Wes goes over his plans. He yanks hard to tighten one particularly stubborn cord. “**A Praxeum ship, huh? The ExploCorps has been pretty secretive to where they've been dispatching them with the war. They're outside the jurisdiction of the navy so they're not even used as part of the war effort.**” Pausing for a moment to study his work he glances over at Wes before spotting Silas himself and getting back to work. 

Silas moves to collect his bag where he'd dropped it once the cargo has been secured. He pauses at the door as Wes asks his question and indicates he should follow him deeper into the ship. “**Arek and Marina will determine that.**” He tosses his bag into a locker on his way to the lounge where passengers can ultimately stay safely out of the way. The engines thrum to life as Silas takes a seat and motions for Wes to join him. 

Veva follows behind but rather than sitting, starts rifling through the galley's cabinets in search of something to eat. Finally content with some sort of snack he collapses into one of the free chairs.

They remain in companionable silence or at least as much silence as can be had by the increasingly thrum of the engines until a gentle shift indicates the ship is lifting off. The noise decreases as the ship leaves the atmosphere.

## **yogi_001** (04/29/2024 17:58:18) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1234564433976758323"></a>*1234564433976758323*

With help from Silas the rest of the cargo was secured rather quickly.  The three of them find seats in the lounge.   Veva even manages to grab some food before they can feel the power from the ship's engines and repulses.


Wes sat in silence as he went through the calming technique he usually did.   The rumble of the ship quickly smoothed out as they made the transition from atmosphere to space.  Wes felt the strange difference in the Force.   It was cold off the planet.  It was a much different feeling than being on a planet where life was abundant.  


Taking a deep breath he let it out slowly and nodded at Silas.   **”Any idea on the time frame of the jump?”**  He wanted to know just as much as he didn’t want to know.    One thing was for sure.   He didn’t want to waste the time he had left with Rin.  He knew they couldn’t be like they were when alone but he still wanted to be around her.  Avoidance and not dealing with it would only be disadvantageous for them both.

## **aliciagd** (05/20/2024 23:30:02) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1242258064669933709"></a>*1242258064669933709*

Rin shifts slightly and straightens as she gets into a more comfortable position in preparation of meditating. Returning his smile, she lets their conjoined hands fall between them, neither wanting to let go of the other. “**I think we can allow ourselves that indulgence.**” Giving his hand a gentle squeeze, she closes her eyes and her body begins to relax into the familiar meditative state.

The thrumming of the hyperdrive blocks out all outside distraction allowing the pair to focus on the meditation. A gentle tingle rises up their arms from their interlocked fingers, an anchor to their physical bodies and each other. Drawn in together by their connection through the Force, Wes finds himself in a white space with Rin standing before him several paces away. Her back is to him as she looks out at something only she can see in the distance of the space. Her hair is half pulled back into a braid and as she turns her head to glance at Wes over her shoulder he can see her Padawan braid moving with her. Rin gives him a small smile, but then her attention turns back to look into the white expanse.

## **yogi_001** (05/22/2024 01:48:35) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1242655318933241946"></a>*1242655318933241946*

Wes opens his eyes.  The sound and vibration that he had felt from the hyperdrive was no longer present.   The room, if it was a room, was completely white.  It lacked any dimension to gauge its size.  


The one thing he could see was Rin, standing several steps ahead of him.  Looking in the direction she is, he sees only white.  Unsure on what to do he steps forward to stand next to her.   He looked over at Rin and she gave him a smile before looking back out into the white.  He turned his gaze back out into the white.  


It was a while until an image started to merge.   Home and then a sudden feeling of loss and despair.  It was crushing.  A young woman needing help.  There was a sense of familiarity about her.  Anger towards him followed by an understanding.  He felt sadness as if something or someone important to him was gone.   He tried to ask the young woman who she was but she simply gave him a small smile and nodded.  The scene once again faded into white. 


He looked over at Rin who was still looking out at whatever she saw in the white void.  Her smile was gone.  Replaced with determination.    He reached out and took her hand into his.   He felt the reassuring tingle and the white slowly faded only to be replaced by the sound and vibration of the hyperdrive.  


He wasn’t sure how much time had passed yet he still felt Rin’s hands in his and he could feel her presence.   It was calm and comforting.   Despite his eyes still being closed he smiled and reached out to her tenitavely with the Force.

## **aliciagd** (05/29/2024 19:09:26) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1245453974086221885"></a>*1245453974086221885*

Time slips by in the peace of meditation. Wes’ awareness of what’s around him comes and goes with his concentration in his meditation. After an indeterminable amount of, Wes comes back to himself only to find he’s alone in the engineering bay. At some point Rin has managed to slip out without him sensing or feeling her departure. Through the Force he gets a sense of where she’s gone, her presence lit like a beacon.

He hears the sounds of lightsabers long before he sees Rin and Veva in the cargo bay. They’ve moved aside some of the crates the best they could to make room for their sparring match. Both of their emerald blades hum at a higher pitch than Wes is familiar with as they dance around each other in the close quarters. The exchange of strikes and parries goes by in a blur as their speed increases. Rin seems to have taken on a more defensive stance, her movements controlled as she blocks Veva’s more aggressive strikes aside and only striking when Veva leaves himself open. 

During one offensive, Rin manages to knock Veva’s lightsaber out of his hand, the weapon turning off as it hits the bulk head and starts to roll away. He tumbles past Rin in a surprisingly agile, acrobatic feat to get out of the path of her blade as he uses the Force to call it back to his hand. Moving too late to intervene, her own attempt to call his lightsaber to her falls short as it springs to his hand. He activates his lightsaber in one smooth action twisting around her to strike. Their blades clash together as the twin green blades meet in a sudden standoff.

After a moment they disengage, both taking a step back from each other and turning off their lightsabers. “**You’ve been practicing Soresu?**” Veva asks and gets a small shrug with a self-satisfied smile from Rin in response. 
“**And you’re relying too much on Ataru,**” she counters. “**Especially in this small space.**” Her head turns slightly towards Wes, acknowledging the presence of their spectator.

## **aliciagd** (06/09/2024 22:11:20) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1249486016440569968"></a>*1249486016440569968*

Rin watches Wes as he sets about writing down the instructions. As he steps closer folding the paper she sits up to look up at him. Finally, she breaks the spell, letting her hands fall to her lap and looks down at the folded paper he had given her. “**Why do I get the feeling you're giving me clan secrets?**” She glances back up at him, reluctant to accept the contents regardless of the fact they were a means for them to keep in touch. Not if it meant putting him at odds with his clan for sharing integral information with an outsider.

## **yogi_001** (06/10/2024 00:01:24) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1249513715817254973"></a>*1249513715817254973*

Wes smiled when she repeated his words as he felt her emotions reach out to him.  He swallowed hard as he stood before her.  Holding her hands he felt the bond tingle between them.   The moment stretched on and he knew he didn’t want to let go.   It was becoming harder as the time grew closer.  


He watched as she blinked the spell away and lowered her hands down into her lap.   It was then that he knew she was the stronger one.  He wasn’t sure he would have been able to let go.   


He followed her gaze to the paper and the information it contained.  Her question and feelings about clan secrets brought forth a half smile as he answered her question.  **”Not all the secrets.   Not even close.  I meant what I said.  You are family now.  With what’s on the paper and my clan's symbol that I gave you on Fakir, if you ever need help, you will get it.”**

---

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (06/10/2024 14:10:15) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1249727336018870423"></a>*1249727336018870423*

With some reluctance Rin nods before folding the paper over once more and slips it in the space beneath her bracer. He had after all told her he’d be giving her a frequency she could reach out to when he had given her the coin. The thought of ever needing the coin in the event she ever needed help left a heavy pit in her stomach; it would mean the Order was no longer there to support her. 

Around them the sounds of the ship changes as the *Aether* drops out of hyperspace and the thrusters take over. Sensing the change, Rin stands. The time for their final goodbyes was upon them. Holding his gaze, she reaches up to touch his cheek with a soft caress. “**I don’t like goodbyes,**” she says. “**There’s too much fanility to it.**” Her hand runs down his arm till she grasps his hand and she gives it a gentle squeeze. “**May the Force be with you,**” she says softly. Before she loses her nerve, she releases his hand and turns back to her bunk to collect her bag and cloak.

---

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (06/10/2024 16:50:44) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1249767723257430147"></a>*1249767723257430147*

Wes felt what he thought was concern as she looked at the paper he had given her.  His hope was that she would never need to use the coin or the message boards he had given her the information for.  He reached out to her with the Force and reassured her that all would be alright.   


The *Aether* shudders slightly as it dropped from hyperspace and a small pot formed in his stomach.   He stood still as she rose to stand before him.   He smiled at her touch.   Her hand was warm against his face.  The tingling sensation from the touch was reassuring.  When she expressed her feelings about saying goodbye he simply nodded as he squeezed her hand in response.  


**”This isn’t goodbye.   This is until next time Cyar’ika.”** 


He gave her a smile as she nodded and said the six words he had heard many Jedi say before.  **”May the Force be with you.”**  it was the first time he had uttered those words.  He was happy that he spoke them to her. 


He squeezed her hand one last time before she slipped it from his grasp and gathered her gear.   He remained quiet as they made their way to the common area where Silas and Veva were waiting.  


Wes walked over to Veva and offered out his hand, taking the young Jedi’s hand when it was offered.  **”Watch your six out there ner vod.”**  Wes said as he called the young man a brother in Mandoa.  


Still having a short time until touchdown, Wes stood to the side so Silas could talk to the padawans in the final moments.

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (06/10/2024 18:36:58) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1249794454743678976"></a>*1249794454743678976*

Silas hasn’t seemed to move from his seat in the common room, though the datapad he’d been engrossed in has been replaced by another. Rin takes a seat near him, letting her bag drop between her feet and her cloak drape across her lap. Setting his datapad down on the table in front of him, Silas then leans in to say something to Rin in a low murmur. She replies back and gets a nod in satisfaction.

Veva is lost in thought leaning against a bulkhead until Wes approaches him and he perks up. He takes Wes’ proffered hand in a firm grip and gives him a grin. “**Will do.**” He inclines his head ever so slightly in Rin’s direction and adds quietly, “**Her’s too.**” Releasing his grip, Veva goes back to casually leaning against the bulkhead and his own thoughts. 

“**Once we’ve dropped off Del-fin we’ll rendezvous with the *Candaressi* for the assault on Tanis,**” Silas is saying to Rin. 
She looks thoughtful as she does the mental calculations. “**We will be in position to take out the defenses by then.**” There wasn’t any doubt in her mind of their success as she spoke. One way or another, they would get the job done.

The sound of the landing struts extending and then the gentle nudge as the ship comes in for a landing in the *Candaressi*’s hanger bay. Silas and Rin stand, but before Rin can gather her things he comes around and places a fatherly hand on her shoulder. He leans in speaking softly. 

Rin listens and then nods. “**Yes, Master. Thank you.**” She collects her things, slipping on her cloak before putting her bag over her shoulder. Her gaze comes to meet Wes’ and with a slow nod of farewell she heads for the cargo bay and the ramp.

As Veva moves to follow Rin, having donned his own cloak and bag, he stops in front of Silas and gives him a polite bow which Silas returns. “**May the Force be with you,**” the Jedi Master says in farewell. Veva responds in kind before giving Wes a nod as he passes to follow Rin. Silas doesn’t move to follow instead taking up his seat once more.

<img src="avatars/352982222636187659/42efdd81c920262f5537ca8c4a23e619.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **yogi_001** (06/10/2024 19:59:15) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1249815165273374720"></a>*1249815165273374720*

Wes gave Veva a small nod as the young Jedi said he’d watch Rin’s back.   They both knew she was capable and that she didn’t need it but it was comforting all the same.   


He listened as they talked about timing and meeting up after they had dropped him off to be with his family.   He quietly wished that Rin could have come with him.  She would have made quite an impression on his father and others in Clan Del-Fin.   


As the *Aether* touched down a feeling of anxiety quietly washed over him as he watched Silas place a fatherly hand on Rin’s shoulder.  Having already said their goodbyes Wes didn’t stop her.   That is until she looked at him and he fought to stay still.  They were both so very close to forsaking their duties.   


Wes nodded slightly and a small smile appeared.  He reached out and gently brushed her with the Force for maybe the last time.   Lost in thought he missed the departure of Veva only seeing the last bit of him as he turned away from the boarding ramp and out of sight.   


Wes felt the boarding ramp begin its ascension as it locked itself back into place.  It was just Silas and him left in the common area.  He let out a breath he found himself to be holding.   Turning around to face Silas who had returned to his seat.   


**”That may have been the hardest thing I’ve ever done.”**  He didn’t expand on what exactly but he figured Silas knew what he meant.  If the Jedi master didn't, that meant he had held his feelings in close.  He was sure he didn’t.  He took a seat across from Silas as the *Aether’s* repulsors came to life and the ship started to ascend into the sky.

<img src="avatars/208916238661844993/d7832f2cac5df42d164b81e35de34f09.png" alt="avatar" style="width: 40px; height: 40px; margin-right: 10px;" width="40" height="40" align="left">

## **aliciagd** (06/13/2024 15:57:54) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1250841589883080798"></a>*1250841589883080798*

Silas folds his hands in front of him as he considers Wes. “**Letting go rarely ever is; especially someone you care about. It's an act of respect and selfless love. **” He pauses for a moment after validating Wes' declaration. “**To mourn is natural, but only by letting go completely will you both be able to find peace. No good will be served by dwelling on what might have been or what might still be.**”

As Silas speaks  the ship jumps to light speed, the multi day journey to reunite Wes with his family has now begun. From the inside pocket of his clothes, Silas withdraws a datacard. “**I”ve taken the prerogative of reaching out to my contacts.**” He holds out the card for Wes to take. “**When you’re ready, there will be a place for you with Master Djinn Altis and his followers. He leads an enclave on Bespin where all are welcome.**”

## **yogi_001** (06/15/2024 13:48:07) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1251533705512620073"></a>*1251533705512620073*

Wes listened as Silas spoke he knew the Jedi master was saying what he believed.  Like most from the order he probably started as a young child not seventeen like he was.   Did that mean anything?   Possibly but like Silas has said, now wasn’t the time to dwell on it.  


Wes felt the ship vibrate as it made the jump to lightspeed and the hum of the hyperdrive settled into the background noise of the ship.  As Silas started speaking again Wes looked up and took the offered data card.  He nodded as he let the info sink in.  The initial plan of the praxeum ship had been changed.  Now he was going to be headed to Bespin.  He had heard of it.   A city in the clouds where they min Tibana gas.   


Wes gave the man a nod.  **”Thank you.  You all have opened my eyes to something that I never would have found on my own.”**  He straightened up and leaned back wondering if Rin knew of the change of plans for him.  He knew the Jedi did things their own way withholding information when it suited their purpose.   He hoped this wasn’t one of those times.  


**”I won’t need a lot of time at home.  You can arrange a pickup for a week after you drop me off.   That will be enough time.”**

He also has no qualms in teaching adults.**”

Wes looked at the data chip again and nodded as Silas spoke.  He gave the Jedi Master a slight smile when he mentioned that Master Altis was a bit more unorthodox in his teachings.   Wes had a feeling that might be what he needed.   The information eased his concern how his future training would intertwine with the training he already had.   While the Jedi train to fight, they weren’t Mandalorian.   


**”Thank you again.  I understand the order is taking a chance with me.   Although I’d wager the order would rather keep eyes on me now that my ability has been discovered than to let me train unsupervised.”**

Silas inclines his head slightly in acknowledgement. “**It will be your decision whether to learn from him or from the Order. There is more than one path to continue your instruction.**” He cocks his head to one side. “**Since you have a holocron you could continue studies on your own, though there's something to be said for learning from another. The Order, while it will take an interest in you, is not in the habit of forcing anyone into following our ways. As long as you don't pose a threat to yourself or others due to your affinity with the Force then you could very well choose to have nothing to do with the Jedi Order. Or even Djinn Altis’ sect of Jedi.**”

## **yogi_001** (06/23/2024 14:34:23) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1254444449719652426"></a>*1254444449719652426*

Wes listened as Silas explained the several different avenues of training could go.  It was good to have options.  Even with the options presented he had a feeling that the order would always have an idea on what he was up to.   


He nodded as he thought for a moment.  **”It won’t hurt to evaluate my options.   They all present pros and cons.   It may just be that they all will benefit me in my training.   Despite my youth I have learned that a singular focus of training can be limiting on what one can learn.”**  


He nodded slightly as his thoughts turned to Rin.   He already missed her and she had barely been gone.  He concentrated and shifted focus.  **”I think. Bespin will be a good start.  I look forward to meeting master Atlis and training with him.  Having said that, I believe I could make use of the three days I have left with you.  Everyone teaches differently.”** Wes gave the Jedi a smile.

## **aliciagd** (06/23/2024 19:00:16) <br style='clear: both;'>

<a name="1254511363980656710"></a>*1254511363980656710*

The journey over the next couple days seems to drag on as Wes spends the time practicing the skills Marina had introduced to the Mandalorian and encouraged him to explore through the holocron. The Jedi Master is open to answering any questions or demonstrating any finer points of the materials Wes comes across. The holocron gatekeeper of Marina's former master, Firith Ven, seems to grudgingly demonstrate or recite any of the knowledge not linked to his personal knowledge regarding Teras Kasi. According to Master Ven, the holocron contains the History of the Galaxy parts one through three, fundamentals to lightsaber form 1 (Shi-Cho) and form 6 (Niman) and numerous holographic recordings by various masters through the ages on Jedi philosophy, history and tactics.

Master Draay returns with Wes to see his father before leaving, turning over the remainder of the payment for the contract including a bonus to account for the additional time Wes had been detained for. He leaves it up to Wes to debrief his father, but will remain should his presence be requested long enough to satisfy any lingering questions. 

A couple weeks later, Marina would send a short letter letting him know of the success of her mission aiding in the take over of the planet Tanis, which its occupation by the Seperatists was impacting the flow of trade for Republic systems along the nearest hyperspace lane. She mentions Veva and a member of a second squad working with them had been injured, but were recovering well. Veva is recalled back to the Temple to complete his recovery, which means he'll be tasked in taking a turn training Younglings (she doesn't know whether to feel sorry for Veva or the Younglings). 
While the Republic secures its foothold on the planet, she's remaining with Master Draay for at least a couple more weeks before they move on. After this message, Wes would get one more a month later, letting him know she's returned to the Praxeum ship *Providence* to catch up on her studies.
